### 11 Rispondi a me; ché le memorie triste

**gemini1-it**

| Italian | Lemma | English | Latin | Interlingua | French | Spanish | Portuguese | Romanian | Esperanto |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Rispondi | rispondere | answer | respondere | responder | répondre | responder | responder | răspunde | respondu |
| a | a | to | ad | a | à | a | a | la | al |
| me | io | me | me | me | me | me | mim | mie | min |

**gemini1-it**
